two clawes yet cheweth cud ād therfore vnclene fleſh ſee ye eate ād carkaſſes ſe ye twych • vnclene theſe ſhall ye eate water ſoeuer hath finnes ſkales water ſees ryuers ſhall ye eate haue finnes ād ſkales ſees ād ryuers moue lyue water ſhall ye abhorre se ye eate fleſh ād alſo ye abhorre carkaſes haue finnes ſcales water ſhalbe abhominacion vnto theſe foules ye ſhall abhorre ſhall eaten abhominacion egle gooſhauke cormoraunte kyte vultur kynd kynde rauens eſtrich nightcrowe cocow ſparowhauke al kynde litle oule ſtorcke great oule backe pellicane pye heron laye kynde lappwynge ād ſwalowe foules crepe ād goo apō iiij ſhalbe abhominacion vnto yet theſe maye ye eate foules moue goo apon iiij fete euen thoſe haue knee aboue vppon fete lepe apon erthe euen theſe ye maye eate arbe kynde soleam kynde hargol kynde ād hagab ād kynd al foules moue ād haue iiij fete ſhalbe abhominacion vnto ſoch ye ſhalbe vnclene whoſoeuer touch carkeſſe thē ſhalbe vnclene vnto euen ād whoſoeuer bereth carkeſſe thē ſhal waſh clothes ād ſhalbe vnclene vntyll euen amonge maner beeſtes haue hoffes deuyde two clawes chewe cud ſhalbe vnclene vnto twicheth ſhalbe vncle ne goeth apon handes amonge maner beeſtes goo foure vnclene vnto many twych carkeſſes ſhalbe vnclene vntyll euen beareth carkeſſe ſhall waſſhe clothes ād vnclene vntyll euen ſoch vnclene vnto theſe alſo unclene amonge thinges crepe apon erth weſell mouſe tode kynde hedgehogge ſtellio licerte ſnayle moule theſe vnclene amonge moue twych dead ſhalbe vnclene vntyll euen ſoeuer dead carkeſſes fall apon ſhalbe vnclene ſoeuer veſſell wodd rayment ſkynne bagge ſoeuer thinge worke wroughte ſhalbe plunged water vnclene vntill euē ſhalbe clene agayne maner erthen veſſell falleth vnclene therein ye ſhall breake maner meate eaten yf ſoch water come apon ſhall vnclene maner drynke drō ke maner ſoch veſſels ſhalbe vnclene whether ouen kettel ſhalbe broken vnclene ſhalbe vnclene vnto neuerthelater yet fountaynes ād welles pondes water ſhalbe clene ſtyll whoſoeuer twycheth carkeſſes ſhall vnclene yf dead carkeſſe ſoch fall apō ſeed vſed ſowe yt ſhall yet clene ſtyll ād yf water poured apō ſeed ād afterward dead carkeſſe fall thereō ſhalbe vnclene vnto yf beeſt whiche ye eate dye twitcheth dead carkeſſe ſhalbe vnclene vn tyll euen eateth ſoche dead carkeſſe ſhall waſſhe clothes remayne vnclene vntyll euen alſo beareth carkeſſe ſhall waſſhe clothes vnclene vntyll euen ſcrauleth apon erth abhominacyon ſhall eaten ſoeuer goeth apon breſt ād ſoeuer goeth apon iiij moo fete amonge ſcrauleth apon erth ſe ye eate abhomynable make youre ſoules abhominable make youre ſoules abhomynable nothinge crepeth nether make youre ſoules vnclene ye ſhulde defiled thereby lorde youre god ſanctified therfore ye maye holy holy defile youre ſoules maner thinge crepeth apon erth lorde brought londe egipte youre god holy therfore holy lawe beeſt foule maner thinge lyueth ād moueth water cōtynue bloude hir purifienge xxxiij dayes ſhe ſhal twytch halowed thinge come ſanctuary vntyll tyme hir purifienge yf ſhe bere maydehilde ſhe ſhalbe vnclene two wekes ſhe hath hir naturall diſeaſe thinge whereon ſytteth ſhalbe vncleane twicheth couch ſhall waſſh clothes ād bath ſelfe water ād vncleane vntyll euen ſytteth whereon ſatt ſhall waſſh clothes bathe ſelfe water vncleane vntill vncleane whoſoeuer twicheth thinge vnder ſhalbe vncleane vnto euē beareth ſoch thinges ſhall waſſh clothes ād bathe hī ſelf water ād vncleane vnto euē ād whoſoeuer twicheth yf haue firſt waſhed handes water muſt waſſhe clothes ād bathe ſelfe water ād vncleane vnto euenynge yf twych veſſell erth ſhalbe broken veſſels wodd ſhalbe renſed water hath yſſue clenſed yſſue let numbre vij dayes one ſynne offerynge burnt offerynge make attonement lord cō cernynge yſſue yf man ſeed departe frō ſlepe ſhall waſſh fleſh water ād vncleane vntill euē clothes furres whereon ſoch ſeed chaunceth ſhalbe waſhed water ād vncleane vnto euē yf womā lye ſoche whone ſhall waſh thē ſelues water vncleane vntyll even whē womās naturall courſe bloud rū neth ſhe ſhalbe put aparte vij dayes ād whoſoeuer twycheth ſhalbe vncleane vnto euē ſhe lyeth apō longe ſhe put aparte ſhalbe vnclene whoſoeuer twicheth hir couch ſhall waſh clothes bathe hī ſelfe water ād vncleane vnto euē whoſoeuer twicheth thinge ſhe ſatt apō ſhall waſſh clothes ād waſhe ſelfe alſo water ād vncleane vnto euē ſo whether twich hir couche thīge whereō ſhe hath ſetē ſhalbe vnclene ūto euē ād yf mā lye meane tyme ſhalbe put aparte well ſhe ād ſhalbe vncleane vij dayes ād couch wherein ſlepeth ſhalbe vncleane woman bloude runneth longe tyme whether tyme hyr naturall courſe longe hir vnclenneſſe runneth ſhe ſhalbe vncleane maner ſhe put aparte hir couch whereon ſhe lyeth lōge hir yſſue laſteth ſhalbe vnto hir couch ſhe put parte ſoeuer ſhe ſytteth apon ſhalbe vncleane hir vnclenneſſe whē ſhe put parte whoſoeuer twicheth ſhalbe vncleane ād ſhall waſſhe clothes ād bathe ſelfe water ād vncleane vnto euen ſhe clenſed hyr yſſue let hyr counte hir ſeuen dayes ſhe cleane viij daye let burne apon alter let caryed forth ſcapegoote waſſhe clothes bathe hys fleſh water come hoſte agayne oxe ſynofferynge goote ſynofferynge whoſe bloude brought make atonemēt holy place let one carye without hoſte burne fyre ſkynnes fleſh ād donge let burneth waſſhe clothes ād bathe fleſh water thē come hoſte agayne ſhalbe ordynaunce euer vnto euē tenth daye ſeuenth moneth ye ſhall humble youre ſoules ſhall doo worke whether one youre ſelues ſtraunger ſogeorneth amonge daye ſhall attonemēt made clenſe youre ſynnes lorde ye ſhalbe cleane ſhal ſabbath reſt vnto ye ſhall humble youre ſoules ſhalbe ordynaunce euer preaſt anoynted whoſe hande fylled myniſtre father ſteade ſhall make attonemēt ſhall put holy lynē veſtimētes reconcyle holy ſanctuary tabernacle witneſſe ād alter youre ſelues ſtraunger ſhall waſſhe clothes ād bathe ſelfe water ād ſhalbe vncleane vnto euē ād thā cleane ād yf waſſhe waſſhe fleſh ſhall beare ſynne ¶ xviij chapter lorde talked moſes ſaynge ſpeake vnto childern iſrael ād ſaye vnto lorde youre god wherfore doynges land egipte wherein ye dwelt ſe ye doo nether doynges lande canaan whether bringe nether walke ye ordinaunces doo iudgemē te kepe myne ordynaunces walke therein lorde youre god kepe therfore myne ordinaunces ād iudgemētes whiche yf man doo ſhall lyue thereby lorde se ye goo none youre nygheſt kyn red vncouer ſecrettes lorde ſecrettes thy father thy mother ſe thou vnheale ſhe thy mother therfore ſhalt thou diſcouer hir ſecrettes ſecrettes thy father wife ſhalt thou diſcouer thy father ſecrettes thou ſhalt diſcouer preuyte thy ſyſter doughter thy father thy mother whether ſhe borne home without thou ſhalt diſcouer ſecrettes thy ſonnes doughter thy doughters doughter thyne awne preuyte thou ſhalt diſcouer ſecrettes thy father wyues doughter ſhe bare thy father ſhe thy ſuſter thou ſhalt therfore diſcouer hir ſecrettes thou ſhalt vncouer ſecrettes thy father ſyſter ſhe thy father nexte kyn thou ſhalt dyſcouer ſecrettes thy mother ſyſter ſhe thy mother nexte kyn thou ſhalt open ſecrettes thy father brother thou ſhalt goo wife ſhe thyne awnte thou ſhalt diſcouer ſecrettes thy doughter lawe ſhe thy ſonnes wyfe therfore vncouer hir ſecrettes thou ſhalt vnheale ſecrettes thy brother wife thy brother preuyte thou ſhalt diſcouer preuytes wife ād hir doughter alſo nether ſhalt thou take hir ſonnes doughter hir doughters doughter vncouer ſecrettes hir nexte kyn therfore wikydneſſe thou ſhalt take wife hir ſiſter vexe hir thou woldeſt open hir ſecrettes longe ſhe lyueth thou ſhalt goo vnto woman open hir ſecrettes longe ſhe put aparte hir vnclenneſſe thou ſhalt lye thy neghbours wife defyle thi ſelfe thou ſhalt geue thi ſeed offer vnto moloch thou defile name thi god lorde thou ſhalt lye mankynde womankynde abominacion thou ſhalt lye maner beeſte defile thy ſelfe therewith nether ſhall woman ſtonde beeſt lye doune thereto abhominacion defile youreſelues theſe thinges theſe thinges theſe nacions defiled whiche caſt lande defiled viſett wykedneſſe thereof apon lande ſhal ſpe hir inhabiters kepe ye therfore myne ordinaunces iudgementes ſe ye commytt none theſe abominacions nether ony ſtraunger ſoiourneth amonge theſe abhominacions haue men lande done whiche lande defiled leſt lande ſpewe ye haue defiled ſpewed nacions whoſoeuer ſhall cōmytt theſe abhominacions ſame ſoules commytt ſhall periſh amonge people therfore ſe ye kepe myne ordinaunces ye commytt none theſe abhominable cuſtomes commytted ye defile youre ſelues therewith lorde youre god ¶ xix chapter lorde ſpake vnto moſes ſayenge ſpeake vnto multitude childern iſrael ſaye vnto holy lorde youre god holye se ye feare euery man father mother ād ye kepe sabbathes lorde youre god ye ſhall turne vnto ydolls make goddes metall lorde youre god ye offre youre peaceofferynges vnto lorde ye ſhall offer ye maye accepted ſhalbe eaten ſame daye ye offer morowe ſoeuer lefte thirde daye ſhalbe burnt fire yf eaten vtmoſt border youre feldes nether ſhalt thou gather left behynd thy harueſt thou ſhalt plucke thy vyneyarde clene nether gather grape ouerſcaped thou ſhalt leaue pore ād ſtraunger lord youre god ye ſhall ſteale nether lye nether deale fal ſely one another ye ſhal ſwere name falſelye thou defileſt name thy god lorde thou ſhalt begile thy neyghboure cauellaciōs nether robbe violently nether ſhall workman laboure abide vntyll mornynge thou ſhalt curſe deaffe nether put ſtomblinge blocke blynd ſhalt feare thy god lorde ye ſhall doo vnrightuouſnes iudgement thou ſhalt fauoure poore honoure helpe ſhed bloude thy neyghboure lorde thou ſhalt hate thy brother thyne hart ſhalt wyſe rebuke thy neghbour thou bere ſynne ſake thou ſhalt avenge thy ſelfe bere hate thy mynde againſt childern thi people ſhalt loue thy neghboure euē thy ſelf lorde kepe myne ordinaunces let none thy catell gendre cōtrary kynde nether ſowe thy felde myngled ſeed nether ſhalt thou put ony garment lynen wollen yf man haue doo woman bonde hath bene medled al another man nether boughte fredome geuen ſhalbe payne apon ſhall dye becauſe ſhe made fre ſhall brynge treſpaceofferynge vnto lorde euen vnto dore mē eate ye ſhal holde vncircumciſed concerning frute euē thre yere ſhal vncircūcyſed vnto ād ſhall eatē id fourth yere frute thē ſhalbe holy ād acceptable lorde fifth yere maye ye eate frute thē ād gather encreaſe lorde youre god ye ſhall eate nothinge bloude ye ſhall vſe witchcrafte obſerue diſmall dayes ye ſhall rounde locke youre heedes nether ſhalt thou marre tuftes thy beerde ye happye art thou iſrael like vnto people art ſaued lorde thy ſhilde helper ſwerde thi glorye thyne enemyes ſhall hyde ſelues thou ſhalt walke vppon hye hilles xxxiiij chapter moſes went frō feldes moab vpp mount nebo toppe piſga ouer agenſt iericho lorde ſhewed londe gilead euen vnto dan nephtali londe ephraim manaſſe ād londe iuda euen vnto vtmoſt ſee ād ſouth region playne iericho citye datetrees euen vnto zoar lorde ſayed vnto lon de ſware vnto abraham iſaac iacob ſayenge geue vnto thy ſeed haue ſhewed thyne eye thou ſhalt goo ouer thither moſes ſeruaunte lorde dyed londe moab commaundment lorde buryed valey londe moab beſyde beeth peor man wyſt ſepulchre vnto daye moſes hundred xx ye olde dyed ād yet eye dym chekes abated childern iſrael wepte moſes feldes moab xxx dayes dayes wepynge mornynge moſes ended ioſua ſonne nun full ſpirite wiſdome moſes put hande vppon childe • n iſrael herkened vnto dyd lorde cōmaunded moſes aroſe prophett ſenſe iſrael lyke vnto moſes lorde knewe face face miracle wonder lorde ſent doo londe egipte vnto pharao ſeruauntes vnto londe myghtye deades greate tereble thinges moſes dyd ſight iſrael ¶ ende fifth boke moſes avims kinde geauntes worde ſignifieth crooked vnright weked belial weked wekedneſſe hath caſt yoke god necke ād obeye god bruterar propheſiers ſothſayers emims kinde geaūtes ſo called cauſe terreble cruell emin ſignifieth terrebleneſſe enack kinde geauntes ſo called happlye becauſe ware cheynes aboute neckes enack ſignifieth ſoch cheyne men weer aboute neckes horims kinde geauntes ād ſignifieth noble becauſe pride called thē ſelues noble gentles rocke god called rocke becauſe ād worde laſteth euer whett thē thy childern exercyſe thy childern thē ād putthem vre zamzumims kinde geaūtes ād ſignifleth myſcheuous waye imaginīge
